itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">0x03. User authentication service</h1><a id="user-content-0x03-user-authentication-service" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0x03. User authentication service" href="#0x03-user-authentication-service"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/895fc5bdbe1a18c2f6fc68ca516b83b3bda327bb0fdf45bfce031c0e3f8c8e0a/68747470733a2f2f63646e2d6270706c6d2e6e6974726f63646e2e636f6d2f4d4a656652774f52766c477a626c657045495249677271514643476c694769472f6173736574732f7374617469632f6f7074696d697a65642f7265762d373266393461652f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f323032302f30372f557365722d41757468656e7469636174696f6e5f2d556e6465727374616e64696e672d7468652d4261736963732d546f702d546970732e6a7067"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/895fc5bdbe1a18c2f6fc68ca516b83b3bda327bb0fdf45bfce031c0e3f8c8e0a/68747470733a2f2f63646e2d6270706c6d2e6e6974726f63646e2e636f6d2f4d4a656652774f52766c477a626c657045495249677271514643476c694769472f6173736574732f7374617469632f6f7074696d697a65642f7265762d373266393461652f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f323032302f30372f557365722d41757468656e7469636174696f6e5f2d556e6465727374616e64696e672d7468652d4261736963732d546f702d546970732e6a7067" alt="" data-canonical-src="https://cdn-bpplm.nitrocdn.com/MJefRwORvlGzblepEIRIgrqQFCGliGiG/assets/static/optimized/rev-72f94ae/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/User-Authentication_-Understanding-the-Basics-Top-Tips.jpg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">In the industry, you should  <strong>not</strong>  implement your own authentication system and use a module or framework that doing it for you (like in Python-Flask:  <a href="https://flask-user.readthedocs.io/en/latest/" rel="nofollow">Flask-User</a>. Here, for the learning purpose, we will walk through each step of this mechanism to understand it by doing.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Resources</h2><a id="user-content-resources" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Resources" href="#resources"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">0. User model</h3><a id="user-content-0-user-model" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 0. User model" href="#0-user-model"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task you will create a SQLAlchemy model named  <code>User</code>  for a database table named  <code>users</code>  (by using the  <a href="https://docs.sqlalchemy.org/en/13/orm/tutorial.html#declare-a-mapping" rel="nofollow">mapping declaration</a>  of SQLAlchemy).</p>
<p dir="auto">The model will have the following attributes:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>id</code>, the integer primary key</li>
<li><code>email</code>, a non-nullable string</li>
<li><code>hashed_password</code>, a non-nullable string</li>
<li><code>session_id</code>, a nullable string</li>
<li><code>reset_token</code>, a nullable string</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. create user</h3><a id="user-content-1-create-user" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. create user" href="#1-create-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will complete the  <code>DB</code>  class provided below to implement the  <code>add_user</code>  method.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&quot;&quot;&quot;DB module
&quot;&quot;&quot;
from sqlalchemy import create_engine
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
from sqlalchemy.orm.session import Session

from user import Base


class DB:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;DB class
    &quot;&quot;&quot;

    def __init__(self) -&gt; None:
        &quot;&quot;&quot;Initialize a new DB instance
        &quot;&quot;&quot;
        self._engine = create_engine(&quot;sqlite:///a.db&quot;, echo=True)
        Base.metadata.drop_all(self._engine)
        Base.metadata.create_all(self._engine)
        self.__session = None

    @property
    def _session(self) -&gt; Session:
        &quot;&quot;&quot;Memoized session object
        &quot;&quot;&quot;
        if self.__session is None:
            DBSession = sessionmaker(bind=self._engine)
            self.__session = DBSession()
        return self.__session
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>"""DB module
"""
from sqlalchemy import create_engine
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
from sqlalchemy.orm.session import Session

from user import Base


class DB:
    """DB class
    """

    def __init__(self) -&gt; None:
        """Initialize a new DB instance
        """
        self._engine = create_engine("sqlite:///a.db", echo=True)
        Base.metadata.drop_all(self._engine)
        Base.metadata.create_all(self._engine)
        self.__session = None

    @property
    def _session(self) -&gt; Session:
        """Memoized session object
        """
        if self.__session is None:
            DBSession = sessionmaker(bind=self._engine)
            self.__session = DBSession()
        return self.__session

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note that  <code>DB._session</code>  is a private property and hence should NEVER be used from outside the  <code>DB</code>  class.</p>
<p dir="auto">Implement the  <code>add_user</code>  method, which has two required string arguments:  <code>email</code>  and  <code>hashed_password</code>, and returns a  <code>User</code>  object. The method should save the user to the database. No validations are required at this stage.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Find user</h3><a id="user-content-2-find-user" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Find user" href="#2-find-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task you will implement the  <code>DB.find_user_by</code>  method. This method takes in arbitrary keyword arguments and returns the first row found in the  <code>users</code>  table as filtered by the methodâ€™s input arguments. No validation of input arguments required at this point.</p>
<p dir="auto">Make sure that SQLAlchemyâ€™s  <code>NoResultFound</code>  and  <code>InvalidRequestError</code>  are raised when no results are found, or when wrong query arguments are passed, respectively.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Warning:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>NoResultFound</code>  has been moved from  <code>sqlalchemy.orm.exc</code>  to  <code>sqlalchemy.exc</code>  between the version 1.3.x and 1.4.x of SQLAchemy - please make sure you are importing it from  <code>sqlalchemy.orm.exc</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
&quot;&quot;&quot;
Main file
&quot;&quot;&quot;
from db import DB
from user import User

from sqlalchemy.exc import InvalidRequestError
from sqlalchemy.orm.exc import NoResultFound


my_db = DB()

user = my_db.add_user(&quot;test@test.com&quot;, &quot;PwdHashed&quot;)
print(user.id)

find_user = my_db.find_user_by(email=&quot;test@test.com&quot;)
print(find_user.id)

try:
    find_user = my_db.find_user_by(email=&quot;test2@test.com&quot;)
    print(find_user.id)
except NoResultFound:
    print(&quot;Not found&quot;)

try:
    find_user = my_db.find_user_by(no_email=&quot;test@test.com&quot;)
    print(find_user.id)
except InvalidRequestError:
    print(&quot;Invalid&quot;)        

bob@dylan:~$ python3 main.py
1
1
Not found
Invalid
bob@dylan:~$ 
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Main file
"""
from db import DB
from user import User

from sqlalchemy.exc import InvalidRequestError
from sqlalchemy.orm.exc import NoResultFound


my_db = DB()

user = my_db.add_user("test@test.com", "PwdHashed")
print(user.id)

find_user = my_db.find_user_by(email="test@test.com")
print(find_user.id)

try:
    find_user = my_db.find_user_by(email="test2@test.com")
    print(find_user.id)
except NoResultFound:
    print("Not found")

try:
    find_user = my_db.find_user_by(no_email="test@test.com")
    print(find_user.id)
except InvalidRequestError:
    print("Invalid")

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. update user</h3><a id="user-content-3-update-user" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. update user" href="#3-update-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the  <code>DB.update_user</code>  method that takes as argument a required  <code>user_id</code>  integer and arbitrary keyword arguments, and returns  <code>None</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">The method will use  <code>find_user_by</code>  to locate the user to update, then will update the userâ€™s attributes as passed in the methodâ€™s arguments then commit changes to the database.</p>
<p dir="auto">If an argument that does not correspond to a user attribute is passed, raise a  <code>ValueError</code>.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
&quot;&quot;&quot;
Main file
&quot;&quot;&quot;
from db import DB
from user import User

from sqlalchemy.exc import InvalidRequestError
from sqlalchemy.orm.exc import NoResultFound


my_db = DB()

email = 'test@test.com'
hashed_password = &quot;hashedPwd&quot;

user = my_db.add_user(email, hashed_password)
print(user.id)

try:
    my_db.update_user(user.id, hashed_password='NewPwd')
    print(&quot;Password updated&quot;)
except ValueError:
    print(&quot;Error&quot;)

bob@dylan:~$ python3 main.py
1
Password updated
bob@dylan:~$ 
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Hash password</h3><a id="user-content-4-hash-password" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Hash password" href="#4-hash-password"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task you will define a  <code>_hash_password</code>  method that takes in a  <code>password</code>  string arguments and returns bytes.</p>
<p dir="auto">The returned bytes is a salted hash of the input password, hashed with  <code>bcrypt.hashpw</code>.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="
bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
&quot;&quot;&quot;
Main file
&quot;&quot;&quot;
from auth import _hash_password

print(_hash_password(&quot;Hello Holberton&quot;))

bob@dylan:~$ python3 main.py
b'$2b$12$eUDdeuBtrD41c8dXvzh95ehsWYCCAi4VH1JbESzgbgZT.eMMzi.G2'
bob@dylan:~$
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>
bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Main file
"""
from auth import _hash_password

print(_hash_password("Hello Holberton"))

bob@dylan:~$ python3 main.py
b'$2b$12$eUDdeuBtrD41c8dXvzh95ehsWYCCAi4VH1JbESzgbgZT.eMMzi.G2'
bob@dylan:~$

</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. Register user</h3><a id="user-content-5-register-user" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. Register user" href="#5-register-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the  <code>Auth.register_user</code>  in the  <code>Auth</code>  class provided below:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from db import DB


class Auth:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Auth class to interact with the authentication database.
    &quot;&quot;&quot;

    def __init__(self):
        self._db = DB()
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>from db import DB


class Auth:
    """Auth class to interact with the authentication database.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self._db = DB()

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note that  <code>Auth._db</code>  is a private property and should NEVER be used from outside the class.</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>Auth.register_user</code>  should take mandatory  <code>email</code>  and  <code>password</code>  string arguments and return a  <code>User</code>  object.</p>
<p dir="auto">If a user already exist with the passed email, raise a  <code>ValueError</code>  with the message  <code>User &lt;user's email&gt; already exists</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">If not, hash the password with  <code>_hash_password</code>, save the user to the database using  <code>self._db</code>  and return the  <code>User</code>  object.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
&quot;&quot;&quot;
Main file
&quot;&quot;&quot;
from auth import Auth

email = 'me@me.com'
password = 'mySecuredPwd'

auth = Auth()

try:
    user = auth.register_user(email, password)
    print(&quot;successfully created a new user!&quot;)
except ValueError as err:
    print(&quot;could not create a new user: {}&quot;.format(err))

try:
    user = auth.register_user(email, password)
    print(&quot;successfully created a new user!&quot;)
except ValueError as err:
    print(&quot;could not create a new user: {}&quot;.format(err))

successfully created a new user!
could not create a new user: User me@me.com already exists
bob@dylan:~$

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. Basic Flask app</h3><a id="user-content-6-basic-flask-app" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6. Basic Flask app" href="#6-basic-flask-app"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will set up a basic Flask app.</p>
<p dir="auto">Create a Flask app that has a single  <code>GET</code>  route (<code>"/"</code>) and use  <code>flask.jsonify</code>  to return a JSON payload of the form:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{&quot;message&quot;: &quot;Bienvenue&quot;}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>{"message": "Bienvenue"}

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Add the following code at the end of the module:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="if __name__ == &quot;__main__&quot;:
    app.run(host=&quot;0.0.0.0&quot;, port=&quot;5000&quot;)
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port="5000")

</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">7. Register user</h3><a id="user-content-7-register-user" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 7. Register user" href="#7-register-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the end-point to register a user. Define a  <code>users</code>  function that implements the  <code>POST /users</code>  route.</p>
<p dir="auto">Import the  <code>Auth</code>  object and instantiate it at the root of the module as such:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from auth import Auth


AUTH = Auth()
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>from auth import Auth


AUTH = Auth()

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The end-point should expect two form data fields:  <code>"email"</code>  and  <code>"password"</code>. If the user does not exist, the end-point should register it and respond with the following JSON payload:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{&quot;email&quot;: &quot;&lt;registered email&gt;&quot;, &quot;message&quot;: &quot;user created&quot;}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>{"email": "&lt;registered email&gt;", "message": "user created"}

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If the user is already registered, catch the exception and return a JSON payload of the form</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{&quot;message&quot;: &quot;email already registered&quot;}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>{"message": "email already registered"}

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">and return a 400 status code</p>
<p dir="auto">Remember that you should only use  <code>AUTH</code>  in this app.  <code>DB</code>  is a lower abstraction that is proxied by  <code>Auth</code>.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">8. Credentials validation</h3><a id="user-content-8-credentials-validation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 8. Credentials validation" href="#8-credentials-validation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the  <code>Auth.valid_login</code>  method. It should expect  <code>email</code>  and  <code>password</code>  required arguments and return a boolean.</p>
<p dir="auto">Try locating the user by email. If it exists, check the password with  <code>bcrypt.checkpw</code>. If it matches return  <code>True</code>. In any other case, return  <code>False</code>.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">9. Generate UUIDs</h3><a id="user-content-9-generate-uuids" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 9. Generate UUIDs" href="#9-generate-uuids"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task you will implement a  <code>_generate_uuid</code>  function in the  <code>auth</code>  module. The function should return a string representation of a new UUID. Use the  <code>uuid</code>  module.</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that the method is private to the  <code>auth</code>  module and should  <strong>NOT</strong>  be used outside of it.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">10. Get session ID</h3><a id="user-content-10-get-session-id" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 10. Get session ID" href="#10-get-session-id"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the  <code>Auth.create_session</code>  method. It takes an  <code>email</code>  string argument and returns the session ID as a string.</p>
<p dir="auto">The method should find the user corresponding to the email, generate a new UUID and store it in the database as the userâ€™s  <code>session_id</code>, then return the session ID.</p>
<p dir="auto">Remember that only public methods of  <code>self._db</code>  can be used.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="bob@dylan:~$ cat main.py

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">11. Log in</h3><a id="user-content-11-log-in" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 11. Log in" href="#11-log-in"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement a  <code>login</code>  function to respond to the  <code>POST /sessions</code>  route.</p>
<p dir="auto">The request is expected to contain form data with  <code>"email"</code>  and a  <code>"password"</code>  fields.</p>
<p dir="auto">If the login information is incorrect, use  <code>flask.abort</code>  to respond with a 401 HTTP status.</p>
<p dir="auto">Otherwise, create a new session for the user, store it the session ID as a cookie with key  <code>"session_id"</code>  on the response and return a JSON payload of the form</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{&quot;email&quot;: &quot;&lt;user email&gt;&quot;, &quot;message&quot;: &quot;logged in&quot;}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>{"email": "&lt;user email&gt;", "message": "logged in"}

</code></pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">12. Find user by session ID</h3><a id="user-content-12-find-user-by-session-id" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 12. Find user by session ID" href="#12-find-user-by-session-id"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the  <code>Auth.get_user_from_session_id</code>  method. It takes a single  <code>session_id</code>  string argument and returns the corresponding  <code>User</code>  or  <code>None</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">If the session ID is  <code>None</code>  or no user is found, return  <code>None</code>. Otherwise return the corresponding user.</p>
<p dir="auto">Remember to only use public methods of  <code>self._db</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">13. Destroy session</h3><a id="user-content-13-destroy-session" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 13. Destroy session" href="#13-destroy-session"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement  <code>Auth.destroy_session</code>. The method takes a single  <code>user_id</code>  integer argument and returns  <code>None</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">The method updates the corresponding userâ€™s session ID to  <code>None</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Remember to only use public methods of  <code>self._db</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">14. Log out</h3><a id="user-content-14-log-out" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 14. Log out" href="#14-log-out"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement a  <code>logout</code>  function to respond to the  <code>DELETE /sessions</code>  route.</p>
<p dir="auto">The request is expected to contain the session ID as a cookie with key  <code>"session_id"</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Find the user with the requested session ID. If the user exists destroy the session and redirect the user to  <code>GET /</code>. If the user does not exist, respond with a 403 HTTP status.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">15. User profile</h3><a id="user-content-15-user-profile" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 15. User profile" href="#15-user-profile"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement a  <code>profile</code>  function to respond to the  <code>GET /profile</code>  route.</p>
<p dir="auto">The request is expected to contain a  <code>session_id</code>  cookie. Use it to find the user. If the user exist, respond with a 200 HTTP status and the following JSON payload:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{&quot;email&quot;: &quot;&lt;user email&gt;&quot;}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>{"email": "&lt;user email&gt;"}

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If the session ID is invalid or the user does not exist, respond with a 403 HTTP status.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">16. Generate reset password token</h3><a id="user-content-16-generate-reset-password-token" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 16. Generate reset password token" href="#16-generate-reset-password-token"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the  <code>Auth.get_reset_password_token</code>  method. It take an  <code>email</code>  string argument and returns a string.</p>
<p dir="auto">Find the user corresponding to the email. If the user does not exist, raise a  <code>ValueError</code>  exception. If it exists, generate a UUID and update the userâ€™s  <code>reset_token</code>  database field. Return the token.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">17. Get reset password token</h3><a id="user-content-17-get-reset-password-token" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 17. Get reset password token" href="#17-get-reset-password-token"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement a  <code>get_reset_password_token</code>  function to respond to the  <code>POST /reset_password</code>  route.</p>
<p dir="auto">The request is expected to contain form data with the  <code>"email"</code>  field.</p>
<p dir="auto">If the email is not registered, respond with a 403 status code. Otherwise, generate a token and respond with a 200 HTTP status and the following JSON payload:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{&quot;email&quot;: &quot;&lt;user email&gt;&quot;, &quot;reset_token&quot;: &quot;&lt;reset token&gt;&quot;}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>{"email": "&lt;user email&gt;", "reset_token": "&lt;reset token&gt;"}

</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">18. Update password</h3><a id="user-content-18-update-password" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 18. Update password" href="#18-update-password"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task, you will implement the  <code>Auth.update_password</code>  method. It takes  <code>reset_token</code>  string argument and a  <code>password</code>  string argument and returns  <code>None</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Use the  <code>reset_token</code>  to find the corresponding user. If it does not exist, raise a  <code>ValueError</code>  exception.</p>
<p dir="auto">Otherwise, hash the password and update the userâ€™s  <code>hashed_password</code>  field with the new hashed password and the  <code>reset_token</code>  field to  <code>None</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">19. Update password end-point</h3><a id="user-content-19-update-password-end-point" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 19. Update password end-point" href="#19-update-password-end-point"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In this task you will implement the  <code>update_password</code>  function in the  <code>app</code>  module to respond to the  <code>PUT /reset_password</code>  route.</p>
<p dir="auto">The request is expected to contain form data with fields  <code>"email"</code>,  <code>"reset_token"</code>  and  <code>"new_password"</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Update the password. If the token is invalid, catch the exception and respond with a 403 HTTP code.</p>
<p dir="auto">If the token is valid, respond with a 200 HTTP code and the following JSON payload:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{&quot;email&quot;: &quot;&lt;user email&gt;&quot;, &quot;message&quot;: &quot;Password updated&quot;}
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>{"email": "&lt;user email&gt;", "message": "Password updated"}

</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">20. End-to-end integration test</h3><a id="user-content-20-end-to-end-integration-test" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 20. End-to-end integration test" href="#20-end-to-end-integration-test"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Start your app. Open a new terminal window.</p>
<p dir="auto">Create a new module called  <code>main.py</code>. Create one function for each of the following tasks. Use the  <code>requests</code>  module to query your web server for the corresponding end-point. Use  <code>assert</code>  to validate the responseâ€™s expected status code and payload (if any) for each task.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>register_user(email: str, password: str) -&gt; None</code></li>
<li><code>log_in_wrong_password(email: str, password: str) -&gt; None</code></li>
<li><code>log_in(email: str, password: str) -&gt; str</code></li>
<li><code>profile_unlogged() -&gt; None</code></li>
<li><code>profile_logged(session_id: str) -&gt; None</code></li>
<li><code>log_out(session_id: str) -&gt; None</code></li>
<li><code>reset_password_token(email: str) -&gt; str</code></li>
<li><code>update_password(email: str, reset_token: str, new_password: str) -&gt; None</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Then copy the following code at the end of the  <code>main</code>  module:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="EMAIL = &quot;guillaume@holberton.io&quot;
PASSWD = &quot;b4l0u&quot;
NEW_PASSWD = &quot;t4rt1fl3tt3&quot;


if __name__ == &quot;__main__&quot;:

    register_user(EMAIL, PASSWD)
    log_in_wrong_password(EMAIL, NEW_PASSWD)
    profile_unlogged()
    session_id = log_in(EMAIL, PASSWD)
    profile_logged(session_id)
    log_out(session_id)
    reset_token = reset_password_token(EMAIL)
    update_password(EMAIL, reset_token, NEW_PASSWD)
    log_in(EMAIL, NEW_PASSWD)
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>EMAIL = "guillaume@holberton.io"
PASSWD = "b4l0u"
